       <div class="homePillars promos acsRow">
        <div class="promo acsCol3 acsCol6Tablet acsCol12Mobile">
         <h3>
          <a href="/member-services" id="content_element_0_home_pillar_row_0_TitleLink">
           Member Services
           <i class="fa fa-chevron-right fa-light">
           </i>
          </a>
         </h3>
         <p>
         </p>
         <p>
          Membership in the American College of Surgeons (ACS) is an integral part of your profession. Whether you're still in training, or at the peak of your career, our top priority is providing value for you, our membersâ€”at every step.
         </p>
        </div>
        <div class="promo acsCol3 acsCol6Tablet acsCol12Mobile">
         <h3>
          <a href="/quality-programs" id="content_element_0_home_pillar_row_1_TitleLink">
           Quality Programs
           <i class="fa fa-chevron-right fa-light">
           </i>
          </a>
         </h3>
         <p>
         </p>
         <p>
          Improving the quality of surgical care leads to greater access for patients, fewer complications and better outcomes, thus lowering the cost of care. Our quality improvement programs have improved quality in trauma and cancer care, bariatric surgery, and in overall surgical care.
         </p>
        </div>
        <div class="promo acsCol3 acsCol6Tablet acsCol12Mobile">
         <h3>
          <a href="/education" id="content_element_0_home_pillar_row_2_TitleLink">
           Education
           <i class="fa fa-chevron-right fa-light">
           </i>
          </a>
         </h3>
         <p>
         </p>
         <p>
          Educating and training surgeons remains integral across the entire spectrum of College activities.  Rely on the ACS to be your premier source for surgical education and take advantage of a wide variety of resources appropriate for your learning needs.
         </p>
        </div>
        <div class="promo acsCol3 acsCol6Tablet acsCol12Mobile">
         <h3>
          <a href="/advocacy" id="content_element_0_home_pillar_row_3_TitleLink">
           Advocacy
           <i class="fa fa-chevron-right fa-light">
           </i>
          </a>
         </h3>
         <p>
         </p>
         <p>
          ACS advocacy activities at the federal and state level represent the interests of you, the practicing surgeon, and your patients.Â  We encourage all surgeons to get involved in advocacy matters. Take action. Protect your patients and your profession.
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>

         <p>
          In response to the enduring need to further decrease sharps injuries, the International Safety Center last year released a consensus statement, Moving the Sharps Safety in Healthcare Agenda Forward in the United States: 2020 Consensus Statement and Call to Action.
         </p>
